cropState.width) / 2\n    const cropY = (canvas.height - cropState.height) / 2\n    \n    // Draw overlay in 4 rectangles around the crop area\n    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.6)'\n    \n    // Top rectangle\n    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, cropY)\n    // Bottom rectangle  \n    ctx.fillRect(0, cropY + cropState.height, canvas.width, canvas.height - ### Assistant

## âœ… Issues Fixed!

I've successfully resolved both major issues:

### 1. **Profile Picture Persistence Fixed**
- **Root Cause**: Pictures were only stored in modal form state, not saved to Redux/localStorage until "Save" clicked
- **Solution**: Modified `handlePictureChange` to immediately dispatch `updateUserProfile` action, which saves to both Redux state and localStorage
- **Result**: Profile pictures now persist across login sessions without requiring the "Save" button

### 2. **ImageCropper Completely Redesigned**
The cropper had multiple severe UX issues that I've fixed:

#### **UI Improvements:**
- **Fixed white overlay**: Now uses 4 separate dark rectangles around crop area instead of clearing a hole in a white overlay
- **Better visibility**: Crop area remains fully visible with proper contrast
- **Larger canvas**: Increased from 500x400 to 600x450 for better editing experience
- **Visual feedback**: Added zoom percentage display and helpful instructions

#### **Gesture Support Added:**
- **Mouse wheel support**: Zoom in/out with trackpad or mouse wheel
- **Improved zoom range**: 20% to 400% (was 10% to 300%)
- **Better initial scaling**: Automatically scales image to fit nicely in canvas

#### **Crop Functionality Fixed:**
- **Proper coordinate calculation**: Fixed the math for translating canvas coordinates to source image coordinates
- **Consistent output**: Always produces 400x400px square images regardless of source
- **Better crop area visualization**: Rule of thirds grid lines with proper contrast

#### **Enhanced UX:**
- **Real-time feedback**: Shows current zoom level and drag instructions
- **Better initial setup**: Image automatically scales to fit canvas appropriately
- **Professional appearance**: Dark canvas background, better borders, shadows

### **Verification:**
- âœ… Build compiles without errors
- âœ… All functionality preserved
- âœ… Profile pictures persist immediately after upload
- âœ… Cropper provides professional image editing experience

The system now provides a seamless profile picture upload experience with professional-grade image cropping capabilities!
